```
                                                                                                                                                                                38
                                                                                                                                                                               39 \left[\mathbf{Q}_{\sigma}\right]_{2} := \left[\mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{s}}\mathbf{B} - \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{t}}(\mathbf{K}_{0} + \mathsf{hv}\mathbf{K}_{1})\mathbf{B}\right]_{2}
                                                                                                                                                                               40 \pi' := (\mathbf{z_A}, \mathbf{C_w}, \mathbf{C_k}, \mathbf{C_t}, \mathbf{C_s},
                                                                                                                                                                                                                           \{\mathbf{P_A},\mathbf{P_d},\mathbf{P_x},\{\mathbf{P_t^j},\mathbf{Q_t^j}\}_{j\in[2k]},\mathbf{Q}_{\sigma}\}
                                                                                                                                                                               41 return \pi = (\left[\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star}\right]_{1}, \left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star}\right]_{1}, \pi_{\mathbf{t}}, \pi')
```

<span id="page-54-0"></span>Fig. 17. Construction of the simulator  $\mathcal{S} = (\mathsf{SSetup}, \mathsf{Sim})$  for the unbounded special simulation sound tLM-NIZK proof system  $\Pi_{\mathsf{U}}$ .

*Proof.* We present the construction of the simulator S = (SSetup, Sim) in Figure 13. We first observe that the crs generated by SSetup is identical to the one generated by Setup in the real scheme.

We prove the zero-knowledge property of  $\Pi_{OT}$  by introducing hybrid games  $G_0, \ldots, G_5$ , where in  $G_0$  the adversary interacts with the real proof system, and in  $G_5$  the adversary interacts with the simulated proof system. We show that the view of the adversary in  $G_0$  and  $G_5$  are computationally indistinguishable. The pseudocode of the hybrid games is given in Figure 18.

**Game G**<sub>0</sub>: This is the original security game where  $\mathcal{A}$  interacts with the Setup

{55}------------------------------------------------

```
Alg Setup(1^{\lambda}):
 01 \ \mathbf{D} \hookleftarrow \mathcal{D}_k
 02 \mathbf{z} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_\mathsf{p}^{k+1} \setminus \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D})\right)
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_1
03 \mathbf{v}_0 \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_\mathsf{p}^k\right); \ \mathbf{z} := \mathbf{D}\mathbf{v}_0
04 \mathbf{z} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_\mathsf{p}^{k+1} \setminus \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D})\right)
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_1-\mathbf{G}_3
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_4
 05 \mathbf{B} \hookleftarrow \mathcal{D}_k; \mathbf{K} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_\mathsf{p}^{2 \times (k+1)}\right); \mathbf{C} = \mathbf{K}\mathbf{B}
 \text{06 crs} := (\left[\mathbf{D}\right]_2, \left[\mathbf{z}\right]_2, \left[\mathbf{B}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_1, \left[\mathbf{C}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_1)
  07 simK := (\mathbf{K}, \mathbf{v}_0)
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_1-\mathbf{G}_3
  08 simK := (\mathbf{K})
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_4
  09 return crs
 Alg Prove(crs, x, w):
 \frac{1 - \mathbf{G}^{k+1} \cdot \mathbf{K}^{k+1}}{10 \ \bar{\mathbf{k}}^{k}} \longleftrightarrow \mathbf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_{p}^{k+1}\right); \ \left[\bar{\mathbf{A}}^{k}\right]_{1} = \left[\bar{\mathbf{A}}_{i}\right]_{1} - (\bar{\mathbf{k}}^{k})^{\mathsf{T}}\left[\bar{\mathbf{A}}\right]_{1}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_3-\mathbf{G}_4
11 \left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star}\right]_{1} = \left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}_{i}\right]_{1} - (\bar{\mathbf{k}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}} \left[\bar{\mathbf{x}}\right]_{1}
12 \mathsf{hv} := \mathsf{H}(\left[\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star}\right]_{1}, \left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star}\right]_{1}, \mathsf{t}); \ \sigma := \mathbf{K}^{\mathsf{T}} \left(\frac{1}{\mathsf{hv}}\right)
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  \mathbf{G}_3-\mathbf{G}_4
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_3-\mathbf{G}_4
 13 \mathbf{v}_{\sigma} \leftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_{\mathsf{p}}^{k}\right); \ \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}\right]_{2}^{1} := \left[\mathbf{D}\right]_{2} \mathbf{v}_{\sigma}; \ \left[\mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}\right]_{2} := \left[\mathbf{z}\right]_{2} - \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}\right]_{2}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                /\!/ \mathbf{G}_0
 14 \mathbf{v_A} := \mathbf{v} - \mathbf{v_\sigma}
15 \mathbf{R_w} \leftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_\mathsf{p}^{k \times k}\right); \ \mathbf{R_k}, \mathbf{R_\sigma} \leftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_\mathsf{p}^{k+1 \times k}\right)
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                \# \mathbf{G}_1-\mathbf{G}_4
 16 \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{w}}\right]_{2} := \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}} \left[\mathbf{D}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2} + \mathbf{w} \left[\mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_1
 17 \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{w}}\right]_{2}^{2} := \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}} \left[\mathbf{D}^{\intercal}\right]_{2}^{2}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_2-\mathbf{G}_4
 18 \left[\mathbf{C_{k}}\right]_{2}^{2} := \mathbf{R_{k}} \left[\mathbf{D}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2}^{2}; \left[\mathbf{C}_{\sigma}\right]_{2} := \mathbf{R}_{\sigma} \left[\mathbf{D}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2}                                    
 20 \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{A}}\right]_{1}^{2} := \left[\mathbf{A}_{i}\right]_{1}^{2} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}}^{2}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_1
\begin{vmatrix} 21 & \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{A}} \end{bmatrix}_{1}^{1} := \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{A}_{i} \end{bmatrix}_{1}^{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}} - \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{x} \end{bmatrix}_{1} \mathbf{v}_{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}} \\ 22 & \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{d}} \end{bmatrix}_{1} := (\begin{bmatrix} \underline{\mathbf{A}}_{i}^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_{1} - \begin{bmatrix} (\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}})^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_{1}) \mathbf{v}^{\mathsf{T}} - \begin{bmatrix} \bar{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}} \\ 23 & \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{d}} \end{bmatrix}_{1} := - \begin{bmatrix} \bar{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}} \end{vmatrix}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_2-\mathbf{G}_4
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_2
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_3-\mathbf{G}_4
 24 \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathsf{x}}\right]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} := \left(\left[\underline{\mathsf{x}}_{i}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} - \left[\left(\underline{\mathsf{x}}^{\mathsf{\star}}\right)^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}\right)\mathbf{v}^{\mathsf{T}} - \left[\bar{\mathsf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}\mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_2
 25 \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathsf{x}}\right]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} := -\left[\bar{\mathsf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  \mathbf{G}_3-\mathbf{G}_4
 26 \left[\mathbf{P}_{\sigma}\right]_{1}^{T} := \left[\mathbf{B}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}^{T} \mathbf{R}_{\sigma} - \left[\mathbf{C}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}^{T} \begin{pmatrix} 1 \\ \mathsf{hv} \end{pmatrix} \mathbf{v}^{\mathsf{T}}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_2
 27 \ \left[\mathbf{P}_{\sigma}\right]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} := \left[\mathbf{B}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} \mathbf{R}_{\sigma}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_3-\mathbf{G}_4
 28 \pi := (\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}} \end{bmatrix}_{1}, \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{w}} \end{bmatrix}_{2}, \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}} \end{bmatrix}_{2}, \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C}_{\sigma} \end{bmatrix}_{2}, \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{A}} \end{bmatrix}_{1}, \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{d}} \end{bmatrix}_{1}, \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\sigma} \end{bmatrix}_{1})
   29 return \tau
```

<span id="page-55-0"></span>Fig. 18. Hybrid games in proving the zero-knowledge property of one-time special simulation sound tLM-NIZK proof system.

and Prove oracles.

$$\mathsf{pr}_0 = \Pr \bigl[ \mathcal{A}^{\mathcal{O}_{\mathsf{Prove}}}(1^{\lambda}, \mathsf{crs}) = 1 \ \bigr| \, \mathsf{crs} \overset{\hspace{0.1em}\mathsf{\scriptscriptstyle\$}}{\leftarrow} \, \mathsf{Setup}(1^{\lambda}) \, \bigr].$$

<u>Game G<sub>1</sub>:</u> In this game, instead of sample **z** uniformly at random from  $\mathbb{Z}_p^{k+1} \setminus \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D})$ , we first sample  $\mathbf{v}_0$  and set  $\mathbf{z} = \mathbf{D}\mathbf{v}_0$ . The only difference between  $\mathbf{G}_2$ 

{56}------------------------------------------------

and  $G_1$  is the distribution of z, it reduce to the  $\mathcal{D}_k$ -MDDH problem.

$$|\mathsf{pr}_1 - \mathsf{pr}_0| \leq \mathsf{Adv}_{\mathbb{G}_1,\mathcal{B}}^{\mathcal{D}_k\text{-MDDH}}(\lambda).$$

<u>Game G<sub>2</sub>:</u> In game G<sub>2</sub>, we change the way of computing  $[\mathbf{C_w}]_2$  and  $[\mathbf{P_A}]_1$ . In the previous game, we have

$$\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C_w} \end{bmatrix}_2 = \mathbf{R_w} \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{D}^{\intercal} \end{bmatrix}_2 + \mathbf{w} \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}^{\intercal} \end{bmatrix}_2, \qquad \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P_A} \end{bmatrix}_1 = \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{A} \end{bmatrix}_1 \mathbf{R_w}.$$

We compute them in  $G_2$  as follows:

$$\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{w}} \end{bmatrix}_2 = \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}} \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{D}^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_2, \qquad \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{A}} \end{bmatrix}_1 = \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{A} \end{bmatrix}_1 \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}} - \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{x} \end{bmatrix}_1 \mathbf{v}_{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}},$$

where  $\mathbf{v_A} = \mathbf{v_0} - \mathbf{v_{\sigma}}$ . Since we have  $\mathbf{z_A} = \mathbf{D}\mathbf{v_A}$ , the change in  $\mathbf{G}_2$  can be seen as changing  $\mathbf{R_w}$  to  $\mathbf{R_w} - \mathbf{w}\mathbf{v_A}^{\mathsf{T}}$ . Therefore, we have

$$|pr_2 - pr_1| = 0.$$

<u>Game G<sub>3</sub></u>: We change the way of computing  $[\mathbf{C_k}]_2$ ,  $[\mathbf{C_\sigma}]_2$ ,  $[\mathbf{P_d}]_1$ ,  $[\mathbf{P_x}]_1$ ,  $[\mathbf{P_\sigma}]_1$  in  $\mathbf{G_3}$ . We first compute two row vectors  $[\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star}]_1$  and  $[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star}]_1$  and their hash value hv, then compute the one-time signature  $\sigma = \mathbf{K}^{\intercal}(\frac{1}{\mathsf{hv}})$ . We recall that in  $\mathbf{G_3}$ , we have

$$\begin{split} \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\right]_{2} &= \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}} \left[\mathbf{D}^{\intercal}\right]_{2}, \\ \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{d}}\right]_{1} &= \left(\left[\underline{\mathbf{A}}_{i}^{\intercal}\right]_{1} - \left[\left(\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star}\right)^{\intercal}\right]_{1}\right)\mathbf{v}^{\intercal} - \left[\bar{\mathbf{A}}^{\intercal}\right]_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}}, \\ \left[\mathbf{P}_{\times}\right]_{1} &= \left(\left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}_{i}^{\intercal}\right]_{1} - \left[\left(\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star}\right)^{\intercal}\right]_{1}\right)\mathbf{v}^{\intercal} - \left[\bar{\mathbf{x}}^{\intercal}\right]_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}}, \\ \left[\mathbf{P}_{\sigma}\right]_{1} &= \left[\mathbf{B}^{\intercal}\right]_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\sigma} - \left[\mathbf{C}^{\intercal}\right]_{1} \begin{pmatrix} 1 \\ \mathsf{hv} \end{pmatrix} \mathbf{v}^{\intercal}. \end{split}$$

We compute them in  $G_3$  as follows:

$$\begin{split} \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\right]_{2} &= \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}} \left[\mathbf{D}^{\intercal}\right]_{2} + \mathbf{k}^{\star} \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\intercal}\right]_{2}, \\ \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{d}}\right]_{1} &= -\left[\bar{\mathbf{A}}^{\intercal}\right]_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}}, \\ \left[\mathbf{P}_{\sigma}\right]_{1} &= \left[\mathbf{B}^{\intercal}\right]_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\sigma}. \end{split} \qquad \begin{aligned} \left[\mathbf{C}_{\sigma}\right]_{2} &= \mathbf{R}_{\sigma} \left[\mathbf{D}^{\intercal}\right]_{2} + \sigma \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\intercal}\right]_{2}, \\ \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{x}}\right]_{1} &= -\left[\bar{\mathbf{x}}^{\intercal}\right]_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}}, \end{aligned}$$

Since  $\mathbf{z}_{\sigma} = \mathbf{D}\mathbf{v}$ , the above change is oblivious to the adversary. Therefore, we have

$$|\mathsf{pr}_3 - \mathsf{pr}_2| = 0.$$

 $\underline{\mathbf{Game}\ \mathbf{G}_{4}}$ : We change again the way of computing  $\mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}, \mathbf{z}_{\sigma}$ . We can observe that in  $\mathbf{G}_{3}$ , we do not use the value of  $\mathbf{v}$  to compute  $\left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\right]_{2}$ ,  $\left[\mathbf{C}_{\sigma}\right]_{2}$ ,  $\left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{d}}\right]_{1}$ ,  $\left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{x}}\right]_{1}$ ,  $\left[\mathbf{P}_{\sigma}\right]_{1}$ . Therefore, we can set  $\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}$  as  $\mathbf{z} - \mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}$  with  $\mathbf{z}$  sample uniformly at random from

{57}------------------------------------------------

 $\mathbb{Z}_{p}^{k+1} \setminus \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D})$ . We can notice that the only change in  $\mathbf{G}_4$  is the distribution of  $\mathbf{z}$ , therefore we have

$$|\mathsf{pr}_4 - \mathsf{pr}_3| \leq \mathsf{Adv}_{\mathbb{G}_1,\mathcal{B}}^{\mathcal{D}_k\text{-MDDH}}(\lambda).$$

Finally, we can observe that Setup and Prove algorithm in  $G_4$  is identical to the SSetup and Sim algorithm. Therefore, we have

$$\operatorname{pr}_4 = \Pr[\mathcal{A}^{\mathcal{O}_{\mathsf{Sim}}}(1^{\lambda}, \mathsf{crs}) = 1 \mid \mathsf{crs} \overset{\hspace{0.1em}\mathsf{\scriptscriptstyle\$}}{\leftarrow} \mathsf{SSetup}(1^{\lambda})].$$

Using the triangle inequality over all above hybrids, we have

$$|\mathsf{pr}_0 - \mathsf{pr}_4| \leq 2\mathsf{Adv}_{\mathbb{G}_1,\mathcal{B}}^{\mathcal{D}_k\text{-MDDH}}(\lambda).$$

Therefore, we conclude the proof.

#### F.2 proof of Theorem 7

**Theorem 7.** The one-time tLM-NIZK proof system presented in Figure 11 satisfies special simulation soundness.

*Proof.* We begin by observing that the vector  $\mathbf{z}$  within the common reference string (CRS), generated by the SSetup algorithm, is designed to lie outside the linear span of  $\mathbf{D}$ . Consequently, either  $\mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}$  or  $\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}$  (or both) must also lie outside the linear span of  $\mathbf{D}$ . This implies the existence of a vector  $\boldsymbol{\xi}$ , which the challenger can derive without affecting the adversary's view, such that  $\boldsymbol{\xi}^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{D} = 0$ , and either  $\boldsymbol{\xi}^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}} = 1$  or  $\boldsymbol{\xi}^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{z}_{\sigma} = 1$ . We consider these two scenarios separately:

- Case  $z_A \notin Span(D)$ : The first verification equation is

$$\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{A}_i \end{bmatrix}_1 \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{w}} \end{bmatrix}_2 - \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{x} \end{bmatrix}_1 \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}^\intercal \end{bmatrix}_2 = \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{A}} \end{bmatrix}_1 \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{D}_2^\intercal \end{bmatrix}_2.$$

Right-multiplying both sides by  $\xi$  yields

$$\left[\mathbf{A}_i\right]_1 \bullet \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{w}} \cdot \boldsymbol{\xi}\right]_2 - \left[\mathbf{x}\right]_1 \bullet \left[1\right]_2 = \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{A}}\right]_1 \bullet \left[0\right]_2.$$

Therefore, in this case, we conclude that  $x \in Span(A)$ .

- Case  $\mathbf{z}_{\sigma} \notin \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D})$ : In this case, we examine the other three verification equations:

$$\begin{split} & (\left[\bar{\mathbf{A}}_{i}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} - \left[(\bar{\mathbf{A}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}) \bullet \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2} - \left[\bar{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\right]_{2} = \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{d}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2}, \\ & (\left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}_{i}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} - \left[(\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}) \bullet \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2} - \left[\bar{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\right]_{2} = \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{x}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2}, \\ & \left[\mathbf{B}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{C}_{\sigma}\right]_{2} - \left[\mathbf{C}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\begin{pmatrix}1\\\mathsf{hv}\end{pmatrix}\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2} = \left[\mathbf{P}_{\sigma}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2}. \end{split}$$

Right-multiplying both equations by  $\xi$ , we obtain

$$\begin{split} \left( \left[ \underline{\mathbf{A}}_{i}^{\mathsf{T}} \right]_{1} - \left[ (\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}} \right]_{1} \right) \bullet \left[ 1 \right]_{2} - \left[ \overline{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}} \right]_{1} \bullet \left[ \mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}} \cdot \xi \right]_{2} &= \left[ \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{d}} \right]_{1} \bullet \left[ 0 \right]_{2}, \\ \left( \left[ \underline{\mathbf{x}}_{i}^{\mathsf{T}} \right]_{1} - \left[ (\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}} \right]_{1} \right) \bullet \left[ 1 \right]_{2} - \left[ \overline{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}} \right]_{1} \bullet \left[ \mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}} \cdot \xi \right]_{2} &= \left[ \mathbf{P}_{\mathsf{x}} \right]_{1} \bullet \left[ 0 \right]_{2}, \\ \left[ \mathbf{B}^{\mathsf{T}} \right]_{1} \bullet \left[ \mathbf{C}_{\sigma} \cdot \xi \right]_{2} - \left[ \mathbf{C}^{\mathsf{T}} \right]_{1} \bullet \left[ \left( \frac{1}{\mathsf{hv}} \right) \right]_{2} &= \left[ \mathbf{P}_{\sigma} \right]_{1} \bullet \left[ 0 \right]_{2}. \end{split}$$

{58}------------------------------------------------

From these equations, we can extract  $\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C_k} \cdot \xi \end{bmatrix}_2$  such that  $(\begin{bmatrix} \underline{\mathbf{A}}_i^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_1 - \begin{bmatrix} (\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}})^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_1) \bullet \begin{bmatrix} 1 \end{bmatrix}_2 = \begin{bmatrix} \bar{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_1 \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C_k} \cdot \xi \end{bmatrix}_2$  and  $(\begin{bmatrix} \underline{\mathbf{x}}_i^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_1 - \begin{bmatrix} (\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}})^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_1) \bullet \begin{bmatrix} 1 \end{bmatrix}_2 = \begin{bmatrix} \bar{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}} \end{bmatrix}_1 \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C_k} \cdot \xi \end{bmatrix}_2$ . Furthermore,  $\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C}_{\sigma} \cdot \xi \end{bmatrix}_2$  constitutes a valid one-time signature for hv. We distinguish between two subcases:

- 1. If  $hv = H([\underline{A}^*]_1, [\underline{x}^*]_1, t)$  where  $[\underline{A}^*]_1$  and  $[\underline{x}^*]_1$  differs from the one generated in the challenge ciphertext, then the adversary has successfully broken the one-time unforgeability of the underlying signature scheme.
- 2. If  $[\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star}]_1$  and  $[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star}]_1$  equals the one generated in the challenge ciphertext, the challenger could have generated  $[\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star}]_1$  and  $[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star}]_1$  as  $[\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star}]_1 = (\mathbf{k}')^{\intercal} [\overline{\mathbf{A}}]_1$  and  $[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star}]_1 = (\mathbf{k}'')^{\intercal} [\overline{\mathbf{x}}]_1$ . Consequently,  $[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}} \cdot \xi]_2 [\mathbf{k}']_2$  equals the  $\mathbb{G}_2$  representation of the re-encryption token from the challenge user to user j.

Therefore, we conclude that the tLM-NIZK proof system Figure 13 satisfies one-time special simulation soundness.

#### F.3 Proof of Theorem 9

**Theorem 9.** The tLM-NIZK proof system in Figure 16 is zero-knowledge. Concretely, for all PPT adversaries A, there exists an PPT adversary B such that

$$\mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{ZK}}_{\mathbf{\Pi}_{\mathsf{H}},\mathcal{A}}(\lambda) \leq 2\mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{MDDH}}_{\mathcal{D}_{k},\mathsf{GGen},\mathcal{B}}(\lambda).$$

*Proof.* We establish the zero-knowledge property of  $\Pi_U$  through a sequence of hybrid games. As the verification algorithm remains consistent across these games, we present only the modifications to the Setup and Prove algorithms for conciseness. The pseudocode for these hybrid games is provided in Figure 19 and Figure 20.

```
\begin{array}{|c|c|c|c|c|}\hline \mathbf{Alg} \ \mathsf{Setup}(1^{\lambda}) \colon \\\hline 01 \ \mathbf{D}_{1}, \mathbf{D}_{2} \hookleftarrow \mathcal{D}_{k} \\ 02 \ \mathbf{z} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_{\mathsf{p}}^{k+1} \setminus \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D}_{2})\right) & \text{$/\!\!/} \mathbf{G}_{0}, \mathbf{G}_{6} \\ 03 \ \mathbf{v}_{0} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_{\mathsf{p}}^{k}\right) \colon \mathbf{z} := \mathbf{D}_{2}\mathbf{v}_{0} & \text{$/\!\!/} \mathbf{G}_{1}\text{-}\mathbf{G}_{5} \\ 04 \ \mathbf{y}_{1} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_{\mathsf{p}}^{k+1} \setminus \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D}_{1})\right) \colon \mathbf{v}_{1} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_{\mathsf{p}}^{k}\right) \colon \mathbf{z}_{1} = \mathbf{D}_{1}\mathbf{v}_{1} \\ 05 \ \left[\mathbf{U}_{1}\right]_{1} = \left[\mathbf{D}_{1} \mid \mathbf{z}_{1}\right]_{1} \colon (\mathsf{svk}, \mathsf{ssk}) \overset{\$}{\hookleftarrow} \mathsf{Sig}.\mathsf{Setup}(1^{\lambda}) \\ 06 \ \mathsf{sim}\mathsf{K} := (\mathsf{ssk}, \mathbf{v}_{0}) & \text{$/\!\!/} \mathbf{G}_{2}\text{-}\mathbf{G}_{6} \\ 07 \ \mathbf{return} \ \mathsf{crs} := \left(\mathsf{crs}' := \left(\left[\mathbf{U}_{1}\right]_{1}, \left[\mathbf{D}_{2}\right]_{2}, \left[\mathbf{z}\right]_{2}, \mathbf{y}_{1}\right), \mathsf{svk} \right) \end{array}
```

<span id="page-58-0"></span>**Fig. 19.** Hybrid security games of unbounded special simulation sound tLM-NIZK proof system  $\Pi_U$  in Setup.

Game  $G_0$ : In this initial game, the adversary interacts directly with the original Setup and Prove algorithms. The winning probability of the adversary in  $G_0$  is therefore:

$$\mathrm{pr}_0 = \mathrm{Pr} \big[ \mathcal{A}^{\mathcal{O}_{\mathsf{Prove}}}(1^{\lambda}, \mathsf{crs}) = 1 \ \big| \ \mathsf{crs} \xleftarrow{\$} \mathsf{Setup}(1^{\lambda}) \big].$$

{59}------------------------------------------------

```
\mathbf{Alg} Prove(crs, t, x, w):

\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_3

\begin{array}{l}
02 \quad \underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star} := \underline{\mathbf{A}}_{i} - (\bar{\mathbf{k}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}} \bar{\mathbf{A}} \ \underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star} := \underline{\mathbf{x}}_{i} - (\bar{\mathbf{k}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}} \bar{\mathbf{x}} \\
03 \quad \mathsf{hv} := \mathsf{H}(\left[\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star}\right]_{1}, \left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star}\right]_{1}, \mathsf{t}) \\
04 \quad \mathbf{v}_{\sigma} \longleftrightarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_{\mathsf{p}}^{k}\right); \ \mathbf{z}_{\sigma} := \left[\mathbf{D}_{2}\right]_{2} \mathbf{v}_{\sigma}
\end{array}

                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             G_4-G_6
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_4
\begin{vmatrix} 05 & \mathbf{v_A} := \mathbf{v} - \mathbf{v_\sigma} \\ 06 & \mathbf{v_A} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_\mathsf{p}^k\right); \ \mathbf{z_A} := \left[\mathbf{D}_2\right]_2 \mathbf{v_A} \end{vmatrix}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_3-\mathbf{G}_4
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         \mathbf{G}_5-\mathbf{G}_6
 07 \left[\mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}\right]_2 := \left[\mathbf{z}\right]_2 - \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}\right]_2
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_4
 08 \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}\right]_{2}^{2} := \left[\mathbf{z}\right]_{2}^{2} - \left[\mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}\right]_{2}^{2}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_5-\mathbf{G}_6
 09 \mathbf{w_t} \overset{1}{\hookleftarrow} \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_p^k\right); \mathbf{t} := \begin{bmatrix}\mathbf{B}_0\end{bmatrix}_1 \mathbf{w_t}; \pi_\mathbf{t} \overset{\$}{\leftarrow} \mathbf{\Pi}_{\mathbf{B}_0, \mathbf{B}_1}^{\lor}(\mathbf{t}, \mathbf{w_t})
 10 \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_{\mathsf{p}}^{k \times k}\right), \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_{\mathsf{p}}^{\ell \times k}\right), \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{t}} \hookleftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_{\mathsf{p}}^{(k+1) \times 2k}\right)
 11 \mathbf{R_s} \leftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_\mathsf{p}^{(k+1)\times(k+1)}\right), \{\mathbf{\Gamma}_i\}_{i\in[2k]} \leftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{Z}_\mathsf{p}^{(k+1)\times k}\right)
 12 \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{w}}\right]_{2} := \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}} \left[\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2} + \mathbf{w} \cdot \left[\mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2}
13 \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{w}}\right]_{2} := \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}} \left[\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_2
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_3-\mathbf{G}_6
 14 \left[ \mathbf{C_k} \right]_2^{\mathsf{T}} := \mathbf{R_k} \left[ \mathbf{D_2^{\mathsf{T}}} \right]_2^{\mathsf{T}}; \left[ \mathbf{C_t} \right]_1 := \left[ \mathbf{U_1} \right]_1 \mathbf{R_t}; \left[ \mathbf{C_s} \right]_1 := \left[ \mathbf{U_1} \right]_1 \mathbf{R_s} \quad /\!\!/ \quad \mathbf{G_0 - G_3}
 15 \left[\mathbf{s}\right]_{1}^{2} = \left[\mathbf{t}\right]_{1} \left(\mathbf{K}_{0} + \mathsf{hv}\mathbf{K}_{1}\right); \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\right]_{2}^{2} := \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{k}} \left[\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2}^{\mathsf{T}} + \bar{\mathbf{k}}^{\star} \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2}^{\mathsf{T}}  // \mathbf{G}_{4}-\mathbf{G}_{6}

16 \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{t}}\right]_{1} := \left[\mathbf{U}_{1}\right]_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{t}} + \mathbf{y}_{1} \left[\mathbf{t}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}; \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{s}}\right]_{1} := \left[\mathbf{U}_{1}\right]_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{s}} + \mathbf{y}_{1} \left[\mathbf{s}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} // \mathbf{G}_{4}-\mathbf{G}_{6}
 17 \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{A}}\right]_{1} := \left[\mathbf{A}_{i}\right]_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_2
 18 \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{A}}\right]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} := \left[\mathbf{A}_{i}\right]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{w}} - \left[\mathbf{x}\right]_{1} \mathbf{v}_{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_3-\mathbf{G}_6
 19 \left[\mathbf{P_d}\right]_1^\intercal := \left[\left(\underline{\mathbf{A}}_i - \underline{\mathbf{A}}^\star\right)^\intercal\right]_1^\intercal \mathbf{v}_\sigma^\intercal - \left[\bar{\mathbf{A}}^\intercal\right]_1^\intercal \mathbf{R_k}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_3
 20 \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathsf{x}}\right]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} := \left[\left(\underline{\mathsf{x}} - \underline{\mathsf{x}}^{\mathsf{*}}\right)^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} \mathbf{v}_{\sigma}^{\mathsf{T}} - \left[\overline{\mathsf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} \mathbf{R}_{\mathsf{k}}
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_3
  21 \left[\mathbf{P_d}\right]_1 := \left[-\bar{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{R_k}\right]_1 \left[\mathbf{P_x}\right]_1 := \left[-\bar{\mathsf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{R_k}\right]_1
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        \mathbf{G}_4-\mathbf{G}_6
   22 for j \in [2k]:
                        \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{t}}^j \end{bmatrix}_1^j := \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{y}_1 \mathbf{t}^\intercal \mathbf{u}_j \mathbf{v}_\sigma^\intercal \end{bmatrix}_1 - \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{U}_1 \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{t}} \mathbf{u}_j \mathbf{v}_\sigma^\intercal \end{bmatrix}_1 - \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{U}_1 \mathbf{\Gamma}_j \end{bmatrix}_1
   23
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_0-\mathbf{G}_3
                                  \begin{bmatrix} \big[\mathbf{Q}_{\mathbf{t}}^j\big]_2 \coloneqq \big[\boldsymbol{\Gamma}_j\mathbf{D}_2^\intercal\big]_2
   24
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             G_0-G_3
                        \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{t}}^{j}\right]_{1}^{2} := \left[\mathbf{U}_{1}\mathbf{\Gamma}_{j}\right]_{1}^{2};\;\left[\mathbf{Q}_{\mathbf{t}}^{j}\right]_{2} := \left[\mathbf{\Gamma}_{j}\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\intercal}\right]_{2} - \mathbf{R}_{\mathbf{t}}\mathbf{u}_{j}\left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\intercal}\right]_{2}

  27 \pi' = (\mathbf{z_A}, \mathbf{C_w}, \mathbf{C_k}, \mathbf{C_t}, \mathbf{C_s}, \mathbf{P_A}, \mathbf{P_d}, \mathbf{P_x}, {\{\mathbf{P_t^j}, \mathbf{Q_t^j}\}_{j \in [2k]}, \mathbf{Q}_{\sigma})}
  28 return \pi = (\left[\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star}\right]_{1}, \left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star}\right]_{1}, \pi_{\mathbf{t}}, \pi')
```

<span id="page-59-0"></span>**Fig. 20.** Hybrid security games of unbounded special simulation sound tLM-NIZK proof system  $\Pi_{U}$  in Prove.

Game  $G_1$ : In  $G_1$ , we change the distribution of z. Instead of being uniformly sampled from  $\mathbb{Z}_p^{\ell} \setminus \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D}_2)$ , we sample  $\mathbf{v}_0$  uniformly from  $\mathbb{Z}_p^k$  and set  $z = \mathbf{D}_2 \mathbf{v}_0$ . Under the  $\mathcal{D}_{\ell,k}$ -MDDH assumption,  $G_0$  and  $G_1$  is indistinguishable for the adversary, and we have:

$$|\mathsf{pr}_1 - \mathsf{pr}_0| \leq \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{MDDH}}_{\mathcal{D}_{\ell,k},\mathbb{G}_2,\mathcal{B}}(1^{\lambda}).$$

{60}------------------------------------------------

<u>Game G<sub>2</sub>:</u> In this game, we introduce a simulation key simK that corresponds to the signing key of the underlying signature scheme and  $\mathbf{v}_0$ . Since this simulation key is generated internally and remains inaccessible to the adversary, the adversary's view remains unchanged. Consequently, we have:

$$|pr_2 - pr_1| = 0.$$

<u>Game G<sub>3</sub>:</u> In G<sub>3</sub>, we first compute  $\mathbf{v_A} := \mathbf{v} - \mathbf{v_\sigma}$ . We can notice that we have  $\mathbf{z_A} = \mathbf{D_2}\mathbf{v_A} \in \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D_2})$ . Then we generate  $\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C_w} \end{bmatrix}_2$  as  $\mathbf{R_w} \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{D_2^\intercal} \end{bmatrix}_2$  without using  $\mathbf{w}$ , and compute  $\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P_A} \end{bmatrix}_1$  using the value of  $\mathbf{v_A}$  as  $\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P_A} \end{bmatrix}_1 := \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{A} \end{bmatrix}_1 \mathbf{R_w} - \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{x} \end{bmatrix}_1 \mathbf{v_A^\intercal}$ . We can notice that when  $\mathbf{z_A} \in \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D_2})$ ,  $\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C_w} \end{bmatrix}_2 = \mathbf{R_w} \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{D_2^\intercal} \end{bmatrix}_2 + \mathbf{w} \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{z_A^\intercal} \end{bmatrix}_2$  is a perfectly hiding commitment of  $\mathbf{w}$ . Therefore, the adversary's view in  $\mathbf{G_2}$  and  $\mathbf{G_3}$  is identical. Thus, we have:

$$|\mathsf{pr}_3 - \mathsf{pr}_2| = 0.$$

Game  $G_4$ : In this game, we generate the proof of the last three equations honestly using  $\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}$  and  $\mathbf{w_t}$ , without using the value of  $\mathbf{v}_{\sigma}$ . Similar to the argument in the previous game, the adversary's view in  $G_3$  and  $G_4$  is identical. Thus, we have:

$$|pr_4 - pr_3| = 0.$$

Game  $G_5$ : In this game, we change the way of generating  $\mathbf{z_A}, \mathbf{z_{\sigma}}$ . Instead of computing  $\mathbf{z_A}$  using  $\mathbf{v_A}$ , we compute  $[\mathbf{z_A}]_1$  as  $[\mathbf{z}]_1 - [\mathbf{z_{\sigma}}]_1$ . Note that the adversary's view is unchanged compared to  $G_4$ . Thus, we have:

$$|pr_5 - pr_4| = 0.$$

Game  $G_6$ : In this game, we change the distribution of z in the Setup algorithm. If there is an adversary in distinguishing  $G_5$  and  $G_6$ , we can construct an adversary  $\mathcal{B}$  that can break the  $\mathcal{D}_k$ -MDDH assumption. We have:

$$|\mathsf{pr}_6 - \mathsf{pr}_5| \leq \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{MDDH}}_{\mathcal{D}_{\ell,k},\mathbb{G}_2,\mathcal{B}}(1^{\lambda}).$$

In  $G_6$ , the adversary's view is identical to the one in interacting with the simulator S. The simulator generates the same crs and simK as in  $G_6$ , and the proof  $\pi$  is generated using the same method as in  $G_6$ . Therefore, we have:

$$\operatorname{pr}_6 = \Pr \left[ \mathcal{A}^{\mathcal{O}_{\mathsf{Sim}}}(1^{\lambda}, \mathsf{crs}) = 1 \mid \mathsf{crs} \overset{\hspace{0.1em}\mathsf{\rlap{\$}}}{\leftarrow} \mathsf{Setup}(1^{\lambda}) \right].$$

Summarizing the above games, we have:

$$\begin{split} |\mathsf{pr}_6 - \mathsf{pr}_0| & \leq \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{MDDH}}_{\mathcal{D}_{\ell,k},\mathbb{G}_2,\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda) + \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{MDDH}}_{\mathcal{D}_{\ell,k},\mathbb{G}_2,\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda) \\ & = 2\mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{MDDH}}_{\mathcal{D}_{\ell,k},\mathbb{G}_2,\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda). \end{split}$$

Thus, we conclude that the tLM-NIZK proof system  $\Pi_U$  is zero-knowledge.  $\square$ 

{61}------------------------------------------------

#### Proof of Theorem 10 F.4

**Theorem 10.** The tLM-NIZK proof system in Figure 11 is special simulation sound. Concretely, for all PPT adversaries A, there exists an PPT adversary  $\mathcal{B}$ such that

$$\mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{SSS}}_{\mathbf{\Pi}_{\mathsf{U}},\mathcal{A}}(\lambda) \leq \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{Unforg}}_{\mathsf{SIG},\mathcal{B}}(\lambda).$$

*Proof.* We begin by observing that the vector  $\mathbf{z}$  is uniformly sampled from  $\mathbb{Z}_{p}^{\ell} \setminus \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D}_{2})$ . Consequently, at least one of  $\mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}$  or  $\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}$  does not belong to  $\mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D}_2)$ . This implies the existence of a vector  $\xi$ , which the challenger can derive without affecting the adversary's view, such that  $\xi^{\intercal} \mathbf{D}_2 = 0$ , and either  $\xi^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}} = 1 \text{ or } \xi^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{z}_{\sigma} = 1.$  Similarly, there exists a vector  $\xi_2$  such that  $\xi_2^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{y}_1 = 1$  and  $\xi_2^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{U}_1=0$ . We analyze these two cases separately:

- Case  $z_A \notin Span(D_2)$ : In this scenario, the first verification equation is given by:

$$\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{A}_i \end{bmatrix}_1 \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{w}} \end{bmatrix}_2 - \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{x} \end{bmatrix}_1 \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{z}_{\mathbf{A}}^\intercal \end{bmatrix}_2 = \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{A}} \end{bmatrix}_1 \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{D}_2^\intercal \end{bmatrix}_2.$$

Right-multiplying both sides by  $\xi$  yields:

$$\left[\mathbf{A}_{i}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{w}} \cdot \xi\right]_{2} - \left[\mathbf{x}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[1\right]_{2} = \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{A}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[0\right]_{2}.$$

Therefore, in this case, we conclude that  $x \in Span(A)$ .

- Case  $\mathbf{z}_{\sigma} \notin \mathsf{Span}(\mathbf{D}_2)$ : In this scenario, we examine the last three verification equations:

1. 
$$(\left[\underline{\mathbf{A}}_{i}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} - \left[(\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}) \bullet \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\right]_{2} - \left[\bar{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2} = \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{d}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2},$$
2.  $(\left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} - \left[(\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}) \bullet \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\right]_{2} - \left[\bar{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2} = \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{x}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{2},$ 
3. For  $j \in [k+1]$ :

2. 
$$([\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} - [(\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}}]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}}) \bullet [\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}]_{2}^{\mathsf{T}} - [\overline{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} \bullet [\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\mathsf{T}}]_{2}^{\mathsf{T}} = [\mathbf{P}_{\mathsf{x}}]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} \bullet [\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\mathsf{T}}]_{2}^{\mathsf{T}},$$

$$\left[\mathbf{y}_{1}\mathbf{t}^{\intercal}\right]_{1}\bullet\left[\mathbf{u}_{j}\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\intercal}\right]_{2}-\left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{t}}\right]_{1}\bullet\left[\mathbf{u}_{j}\mathbf{z}_{\sigma}^{\intercal}\right]_{2}=\left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{t}}^{j}\right]_{1}\bullet\left[\mathbf{D}_{2}^{\intercal}\right]_{2}+\left[\mathbf{U}_{1}\right]_{1}\bullet\left[\mathbf{Q}_{\mathbf{t}}^{j}\right]_{2},$$

4.  $\left[\mathbf{C_s}\right]_1 \bullet \left[\mathbf{B}\right]_2 - \left[\mathbf{C_t}\right]_1 \bullet \left[\left(\mathbf{K}_0 + \mathsf{hv}\mathbf{K}_1\right)\mathbf{B}\right]_2 = \left[\mathbf{U}_1\right]_1 \bullet \left[\mathbf{Q}_{\sigma}\right]_2$ . By right-multiplying  $\xi$  to all three equations and left-multiplying  $\xi_2^\intercal$  to the second equation, we obtain:

second equation, we obtain:  
1. 
$$(\left[\underline{\mathbf{A}}_{i}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} - \left[(\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}) \bullet \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\xi\right]_{2} - \left[\bar{\mathbf{A}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[1\right]_{2} = \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{d}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[0\right]_{2},$$
  
2.  $(\left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} - \left[(\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\star})^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1}) \bullet \left[\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\xi\right]_{2} - \left[\bar{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[1\right]_{2} = \left[\mathbf{P}_{\mathsf{x}}\right]_{1} \bullet \left[0\right]_{2},$   
3. For  $j \in [k+1]$ :

2. 
$$([\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} - [(\underline{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{X}})^{\mathsf{T}}]_{1}) \bullet [\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\xi]_{2}^{\mathsf{T}} - [\bar{\mathbf{x}}^{\mathsf{T}}]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} \bullet [1]_{2}^{\mathsf{T}} = [\mathbf{P}_{\mathsf{X}}]_{1}^{\mathsf{T}} \bullet [0]_{2}^{\mathsf{T}},$$

$$\begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{t}^{\intercal} \end{bmatrix}_{1} \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{u}_{j} \end{bmatrix}_{2} - \begin{bmatrix} \xi_{2}^{\intercal} \mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{t}} \end{bmatrix}_{1} \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{u}_{j} \end{bmatrix}_{2} = \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{P}_{\mathbf{t}}^{j} \end{bmatrix}_{1} \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{0} \end{bmatrix}_{2} + \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{0} \end{bmatrix}_{1} \bullet \begin{bmatrix} \mathbf{Q}_{\mathbf{t}}^{j} \end{bmatrix}_{2},$$

4.  $\left[\xi_2^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{C_s}\right]_1 \bullet \left[\mathbf{B}\right]_2 - \left[\xi_2^{\mathsf{T}}\mathbf{C_t}\right]_1 \bullet \left[\left(\mathbf{K}_0 + \mathsf{hv}\mathbf{K}_1\right)\mathbf{B}\right]_2 = \left[0\right]_1 \bullet \left[\mathbf{Q}_\sigma\right]_2$ . From the above equations, the challenger can derive the vector  $|\mathbf{C}_{\mathbf{k}}\xi|_2$ , which represents a re-encryption token from  $\left[\underline{\mathbf{A}}_{i}\right]_{1}$  to  $\left[(\underline{\mathbf{A}}^{\star})^{\intercal}\right]_{1}$  and  $\left[\underline{\mathbf{x}}_{i}\right]_{1}$ to  $\left[(\underline{x}^{\star})^{\intercal}\right]_{1}$ . Furthermore, the second equation implies that  $\left[\mathbf{C_{t}}\right]_{1}$  is a commitment to  $\mathbf{t}$ , and  $\begin{bmatrix} \xi_2^\mathsf{T} \mathbf{C_s} \end{bmatrix}_1$  and  $\begin{bmatrix} \xi_2^\mathsf{T} \mathbf{C_t} \end{bmatrix}_1$  constitute a valid signature for  $hv = H([\underline{A}^{\star}]_1, [\underline{x}^{\star}]_1, t)$ . Therefore, unless the adversary can break the unforgeability of the underlying signature scheme, the adversary must have derived an invalid re-encryption token.

{62}------------------------------------------------

## <span id="page-62-0"></span>**G Security Proof for Single-Challenge aCCA-Secure PRE**

<span id="page-62-1"></span>**Theorem 15.** *If we instantiate the general construction of* PREaCCA *Figure [6](#page-28-0) with*

- **–** SMP*: a hard subset membership language distribution*
- **–** VSHPS*: a vector space hash proof system* VSHPS *with* (*ε, d*)*-universal, with d* ≥ 1*.*
- **–** OTS*: an one-time signature scheme* OTS *that is one-time strongly unforgeable.*
- **–** tLM*-*NIZK*: an one-time special simulation-sound tag-based language-malleable* NIZK *proof system* tLM*-*NIZK *for the language corresponded to* SMP *and* VSHPS*.*

*Then the resulting* PREaCCA *scheme is single-challenge* aCCA *secure against any* PPT *adversary* A*, with advantage*

$$\begin{split} \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{SC-aHRA}}_{\mathsf{PRE},\mathcal{A}}(\lambda) \leq & \binom{\mathsf{N_U}}{2} \cdot \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{KCol}}_{\mathsf{SMP},\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda) + \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{ZK}}_{\mathsf{tLM-NIZK},\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda) + \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{StUnforg}}_{\mathsf{OTS},\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda) \\ & + \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{Collision}}_{\mathsf{H},\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda) + 2 \cdot \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{SSS}}_{\mathsf{tLM-NIZK},\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda) + \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{HSM}}_{\mathsf{SMP},\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda) \\ & + \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{BadUniv}}_{\mathsf{VSHPS},\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda). \end{split}$$

*Proof.* We prove the above theorem via the following hybrid security games **G**0*, . . . ,* **G**<sup>10</sup> . The detailed security games are presented in Figure [21.](#page-63-0) **Game G**0**:** This is the original SC-aCCA security game. By definition, the adversary's success probability is

$$\mathsf{pr}_0 \coloneqq \Pr \Big[ \mathsf{Exp}^{\mathsf{SC-aCCA}}_{\mathsf{PRE},\mathcal{A}}(1^\lambda) = 1 \Big].$$

**Game G**1**:** This game is identical to **G**0, except that the challenger aborts if a collision occurs among the generated public keys. Let BadCol be the event that there exist distinct *i, j* ∈ [NU] such that pk*<sup>i</sup>* = pk*<sup>j</sup>* . If BadCol occurs, the game aborts.

The difference in the adversary's success probability between these two games is bounded by the probability of the event BadCol. Using a standard union bound argument, we have:

$$|\mathsf{pr}_0 - \mathsf{pr}_1| \leq \Pr[\mathsf{Bad}_\mathsf{Col}] \leq \binom{\mathsf{N}_\mathsf{U}}{2} \cdot \mathsf{Adv}^{\mathsf{KCol}}_\mathsf{SMP,\mathcal{B}}(1^\lambda).$$

**Game G**2**:** In this game, we modify the way of generating the public parameters. Instead of sampling the projection key projk uniformly from the set PKlpk, we first sample the hash key hk using the hash proof system's setup algorithm, then compute the projection key as projk := PKGen(hk*,*Llpk). Since both methods of generating projk yield the same distribution, we have

$$\mathsf{pr}_2 = \mathsf{pr}_1$$

*.*

```
                                                            /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_{5-10}
                                                                                              36 ct_1 := PEval(projk_i, x, w)
                                                                                                                                                                                G_{0-2}
               \operatorname{return} \perp
11
                                                                   G_{5-10}
                                                                                              37 \operatorname{ct}_1 := \operatorname{\mathsf{SEval}}(\operatorname{\mathsf{hk}}_i' + \operatorname{\mathsf{hk}}, \mathsf{x})
                                                                                                                                                                                /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_{3-8}
12 if Bad_{Tag} then
                                                                 G_{5-10}
                                                            38 v \leftarrow \mathsf{U}\left(\mathbb{F}\right)
                                                                                                                                                                         /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_{9-10}
13
               abort
                                                            /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_{5-10}
                                                                                              39 \mathsf{ct}_1 := \mathsf{SEval}(\mathsf{hk}_i + \mathsf{hk}, \mathsf{x})
14 return m
                                                                                                           +v \cdot \mathsf{SEval}(\mathsf{h},\mathsf{x})
                                                                                                                                                                              /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_{9-10}
Oracle \mathcal{O}_{\mathsf{ReEnc}}(i, j, \mathsf{ct}):
                                                                                             40 ct_2 := PEval(projk, x, w) + m
                                                                                                                                                                                //
                                                                                                                                                                                     G_{0-2}
15 if \neg \mathsf{CheckSMP}_{\mathcal{L}}()^{a}
                                                            /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_{6-10}
                                                                                             41 ct_2 := SEval(hk, x) + m
                                                                                                                                                                               /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_{3-9}
               return \perp

                                                            /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_{6-10}

                                                                                                                                                                              \# \mathbf{G}_{10}

                                                            /\!\!/ \mathbf{G}_{6-10}

               abort

               \mathcal{L}_\mathsf{C} := \mathcal{L}_\mathsf{C} \cup \{(j,\mathsf{ct}')\}
```
